 aakhirkaar 1950 main asprishyata par roak laga di gai
 Legal protection against such social discrimination was provided by creating an anti-untouchability law in 1955 and an anti-harassment law in 1989
 isi tarah rojgaar or shiksha main bhedbhaav ke khilaaf suraksha dene ke liye aarakshan kii niti banaai gai taaki unka aarthik or shaikshik str upar uth sake or vidhanmandalon main ye nitiyaan saath saal se bhi zyada samay se chal rahi hai
 Therefore, it becomes imperative for us to ask this question: Is caste-based high-caste and untouchability now become the talk of history? Have Dalits achieved solid economic and educational development? Have they got equal civil rights to others? After all, what has been achieved so far with the political efforts of civil society and Dalits? If we look at the situation before 1950, we can say that their economic and educational situation has changed
 bhedbhaav or asprishyata ke morche par bhi pragati hui he
 But the pace of progress has been much slower than expected
 dalit aaj bhi oonchi jatiyon se bahut peeche hai or garibi or jatigat bhedbhaav kii samasya badastoor jari he
 Although government data and studies show that there has been some improvement in the matter of Dalits gaining civil rights, untouchability continues on a large scale even today
 1995-2014 ke bich jatigat bhedbhaav or atyaachaar ke 2
 43 lakh cases have been registered
 is hisaab se saal main ausatan 13,000 maamle baithte hai
 This is just a hallmark, because only such serious cases are registered
 aarthik kshetra main dekhen to kabhi asprishy samajhe jane vaale daliton ko vibhinn bazaaron main bhedbhaav kaa saamana karnaa padataa he, jinamein shram bazaar bhi shaamil he
 Dalits, considered untouchable in rural areas, are not employed for certain tasks, such as cooks in restaurants and to prepare mid-day meals for children
 yahaan tak ki unhen waiter kaa kaam bhi dene se parhez kiya jaataa he
 They are employed for less days and at lower wages than workers of the larger caste, while they are forced to work for some other jobs
 shaharon main nijee companiyon main agadi jatiyon ke mukaable daliton ko intervyuu ke liye kam sankchaya main bulaayaa jaataa he, bhale hi donon kii yogyataayen samaan hon
 Dalits also face discrimination in buying agricultural land, similarly in the case of rental of houses in cities, Dalits have to face discrimination
 gaiyr-krishi rojgaar or vyapaar ke kshetra main daliton ke saath bhedbhaav bartaa jaataa he
 On the basis of the experiences of 90 Dalit entrepreneurs in 13 districts of 6 states in the country, Aseem Prakash found that SC entrepreneurs and businessmen had to face caste barriers in various markets
 sampatti kii milkiyat ke maamle main 2012 main kul gramin anusuchit pariwaron main se 20 fisadi kisaan the or anya 14 fisadi chote udhyami yaa kaarobaari the, jabaki shahari ilaakon main yah anupaat kareeb 27 fisadi tha
 The 2005 Economic Survey of Private Enterprises shows that the Scheduled Castes had only 10 per cent share in the country's business market, which is much less than their total population
 dalit shiksha or naagarik suvidhaon main hissedari ke maamle main bhi peeche hai
 In 2014, the share of Scheduled Castes in terms of enrollment for higher education was 22%, while the share of upper castes was 42%
 is prakaar jati-aadhaarit bhedbhaav or garibi dikhaati he ki kuch had tak sudhaar ke baavjood dalit aaj bhi bade str par bhedbhaav kaa saamana kar rahe hai
 There is a difference between them and the rest in terms of human development
 ab bhi unhen purna naagarik kaa darja hasil nahin he—ambedkar ke shabdon main ve ''hindu samaaj kaa hissaa hai, lekin bilkul alag hissaa
 “dalits are facing many challenges today
 1990 ke dashak ke shuruaati varshon tak unki pragati kaa bada strot sarkari naukariyon or shiksha main aarakshan hua karata tha
 But due to the rapidly increasing rate of privatization, both of those sources are ending
 is tarah nijeekaran kaa matlab aarakshan khatm hona he
 There has been a sharp decline in government jobs, which is now only 20 per cent, while 80 per cent of the jobs are in the private sector, and there is no reservation in the private sector
 ucch shiksha ke kshetra main nijee vishvavidhyalayon or mahavidhyalayon main padhgaye vaale chaatro kii sankchaya kul chaatro kii sankhya kaa kareeb ek-tihaai he or yahaan bhi koi aarakshan nahin he
 Therefore, Dalits have a very low share in 80% of private jobs and 30% of the education sector
 is prakaar nijee kshetra main unke liye chunautiyaan bani hui hai
 The second challenge is on the political front
 rajnatik aarakshan ne prashasnic or nirnay lene ke kshetra main daliton ko sthaan diya he
 By giving Dalits a stake in the legislature, they contribute to formulating policies in their favor
 lekin unki prabhavi bhoomika kii kuch simaaen hai
 This limitation is due to electoral methods
 dow
 Ambedkar said that the election of Dalits under the electoral system of political reservation depends on the upper caste majority vote
 isse dalit vidhayika kaa prabhaav simit ho jaataa he
 That's why Dr
 ambedkar ne unke liye ek alag nirvaachak mandal kii maang kii thi, jisamen sirf dalit hi apane ummidavaaron kaa chunaav kar saken
 Now the time has come to reform the electoral system, thereby creating an independent Dalit Legislature, which will give them a chance to work independently
 ambedkar ne sansadeey loktantr main alpsankhyakon ke liye kuch suraksha kaa suzav diya tha
 He said that the majority party would not necessarily be secular
 isliye unka suzav tha ki bahumat vaali party ke pradhanmantri or mantri kaa chunaav puure sadan kii ore se kiya janaa chahie, jisamen bahumat or alpsankhyak donon rajnatik partiyon kaa vidhanmandal shaamil ho
 Ambedkar was also concerned about another challenge and that is discrimination of the administrative region dominated by the upper castes
 unka maananaa tha ki is bhedbhaav ke kaaran daliton se sambandhit yojanaon ko lagu karne main samasya aegi
 All government offices have a union of Dalit employees, who constantly fight to implement the reservation policy and other schemes
 ambedkar ne niti-nirmaan or amal karne vaali sansthaaon main dalit adhikariyon kii bhartee ke liye kuch upaay sujhaaye the
 Except for the use of Bahujan Samaj Party in Uttar Pradesh, at the level of a political party, in most states they lack political unity and some are very weak, even in Maharashtra there is no political among them There is no mobilization
 dalit civil socity gaiyr-rajnatik sanghathan ke jariye apane dam par vibhinn staron par kaam karti he, khaskar sarkari karmchaariyon ke bich ek simit agenda ke saath
 There is no organization at the all India level that can make any kind of impact at the level of the whole country
 rohit vemula kii aatmahatya, una or maharashtra kii ghatnaon ke maamle main haal main jis tarah kii jaagrukta or ekta dekhi gai, vah is baat kaa sanket he ki gramin kshetra ke madhya, nimna madhya, nimna varg or yuvaaon main baari chetana ai he
 But there is a lack of a policy agenda to organize them under one umbrella to solve their problems
 daliton kii samasyaayein jatil ho chuki hai, isliye saamaanya tareeke se unhen sangathit karnaa aasaan nahin he
 But the newly shown consciousness awakens the hope for a better tomorrow

 Dear Bashistha brother, the news of giving me an ultimatum to decide in relation to contesting elections has appeared in today's newspapers
 is khabar se main stambhit hum
 It seems that the effect of age on your memory is starting to fall prematurely
 22 janvari kii raat nau-saadhe nau baje ke lagbhag aapane mujhe nitish kumaar kaa farmaan sunaaya tha ki mujhe baxur se chunaav ladanaa he to avilamb maine aapako bataa diya ki main chunaav nahin laduunga
 How can i do the foolishness of contesting on the ticket of a person who cuts a Rajya Sabha card for two other innocents to cut me? My point was proved during Karpoori Jayanti the next day when Nitish challenged his speech during his speech Said that those who say that the party is weak, show it by fighting elections
 jis dhang se party chalaayi ja rahi he usase party kamjor ho rahi he, aisa to sirf maine hi rajgir ke shivi main kaha tha
 So why are NK Singh and Sabir Ali being asked to contest from the Rajya Sabha
 jo aadmi nafrat kii had tak mujhe naapsand karata he, jo mujhe kaatane ke liye do nirdosho kaa nishthurataa ke saath vadh kar saktaa he uski ore se chunaav ladane kii baat main kaise soch saktaa hum
 The extent is in the case of Sabir
 use to ramvilas ji ne rajyasabha main bheja tha
 That same term is ending
 dobaaraa rajyasabha main usko bheja jayega, isi shart par vah hamalogon ke saath aayaa tha
 According to my information, which is confirmed, the last time when Nitish came to Delhi, in front of Sabir and NK Singh at Bihar residence, when someone asked Nitish that the term of Sabir Saheb was ending
 ab inkaa kya hoga
 So Nitish had said in front of everyone that Sabir Saheb will again go to Rajya Sabha
 dilli vidhansabha ke chunaav main sabir kaa kis prakaar dohan hua he yah bahuton kii jaankaree main he
 In which there will be a little bit of humility, how can he deal with her in this way
 main acchhee tarah jaanata hum ki nitish jitaane ke liye nahin mujhe haraane ke liye chunaav ladane ko kah rahe hai
 At the same time when we came out of the NDA, i told Nitish that i wanted to contest the election
 aap ladiye- yah kehane main us samay kya dikkat thi
 Why was the platform of Srikrishna Memorial chosen to declare his decision to contest elections
 faisla sunaane kaa jo andaaj or tevar tha vah chunaav jitaane vaala tha yaa haraane vaala? isi liye parason jab dobaaraa aapane poocha to phir maine inkaar kar diya tha

 Park Ji Sung, South Korea's most talented player, has retired from international football
 england ke club manchester united ke liye peshewar footbal khilne vaale sung ne haal hi main sampann asian cap ke dauraan apane desh ke liye 100waan match khelaa tha
 Korea's team lost to Japan in the semi-finals
 chot ke kaaran sung tisare or chauthe sthaan ke liye khele gaye plaof mukaable main nahin khel sake the
 The South Korea Football Federation has said that Sung has said goodbye to international football after suffering a knee injury
 sung ke mutabik vah chaahate hai ki unke sthaan par kisi yuva ko mauka diya jaae
 Sung, 29, said, "I want to play club football for the next three-four years
 desh ke liye khelnaa mere liye gaurav kii baat he
 i am happy that many talented players have come forward to take my place
 " asia ke sabase safal footbal khilaadiyon main ek sung champiens lig main hissaa lene vaale pehle asian khilaadi bane the
 While on his team, United have won three Premier League, three League Cups and one English club title

 The social fabric is composed of the areas of Angul and Dhenkanal districts of Odisha
 2011 kii janaganana ke mutabik yahaan kii jansankhya 19 lakh 32 hajaar 982 he

 is seat par anusuchit jati kii aabaadi 19

 There are 7 seats of Odisha Legislative Assembly under Dhenkanal Lok Sabha seat
 ye siten hai dhenkanal, prajnga, kamakhyanagar, hindol, anugul, talchar or pallaharaa
 In the 2014 assembly elections, the Biju Janata Dal had a great success in these seats and won their candidates in all the seats
 seat kaa itihaasadhenkanal loksabhaa seat par congress or biju janata dal kaa prabhutv rahaa he
 Janta Dal, Swatantra Party and Republic Council candidates have been winning this seat from time to time
 1952 main is seat par congress candidet niranjan jena ne jeet hasil kii
 In 1957 Surendra Mohanty of Republic Council won the elections
 1962 main ye seat congress ke kabje main ai
 In 1967, Swatantra Party opened an account on the seat
 1971 main yahaan se congress ke devendra satpathi ko vijay shri hasil hui
 In 1977, when there was a wave against the Congress in the country, Devendra Satpathy joined the Bharatiya Lok Dal and won elections on this seat
 1980-84 main dhenkanal seat par congress kaa kabja rahaa
 Kamakhya Prasad Singh Dev won the election both times
 kamakhya prasad singh dev sthaneey raaj parivaar ke sadsy hai or unke parivaar kaa is seat par prabhutv he
 In 1989, there was a wave of change and the public won
 lekin 1991 main congress ke tikat par kamakhya dev ne phir vaapasi kii
 He also won in 1996
 1997 ke aakhri dinon main biju janata dal ke gathan ke baad is seat kaa sameekaran badal gaya
 The Tathagata Satpathy of the Congress emerged victorious in the 1998 Lok Sabha elections
 haalanki 1999 main jab chunaav hue to congress ne yahaan jeet hasil kii
 Since 2004, the Biju Janata Dal has strengthened its hold on this seat
 2004, 09, 14 teenon hi loksabhaa chunaav main bijedy ke tikat par tathagat satpathi yahaan se chunaav jitate rahe hai
